Regulation S-T Rule 101(b)(7) only permits the submission in paper of a Form 6-K
if submitted to furnish a report or other document that the registrant foreign
private issuer must furnish and make public under the laws of the jurisdiction
in which the registrant is incorporated, domiciled or legally organized (the
registrant's "home country"), or under the rules of the home country exchange on
which the registrant's securities are traded, as long as the report or other
document is not a press release, is not required to be and has not been
distributed to the registrant's security holders, and, if discussing a material
event, has already been the subject of a Form 6-K submission or other Commission
filing on EDGAR.</font></font></font></div>

            </td>
            <td valign="top" width="85%">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;
      </font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Company's 2008 financial statements have been audited and attested by

              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;

          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;</font></td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" width="85%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>

            <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;
    </font></td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" width="85%">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Summary
      of shareholders&#8217; comments/questions and Company&#8217;s
  replies:</font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;
    </font></td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" width="85%">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Hu
      X-ming, Shareholder No. 375442, Attendance No. 4:&#160;&#160;The
      percentage of decrease in the costs of goods sold was not consistent with
      the percentage of decrease in sales revenue, while the expenses increased
      instead of decreasing; information on operating costs provided in Notes to
      the Annual Report; the Company&#8217;s&#160;&#160;asset turnover rate dropped
      and there were changes in long-term equity method investment.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Chairperson&#8217;s
      reply: Because of the global economic crisis and financial tsunami in the
      fourth quarter last year, the Company&#8217;s sales dropped, resulting in less
      revenues and rising costs. But the expenses did not increase.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CFO&#8217;s
      reply: Last year for the sake of enhancing the overall business
      performance of the Company, we consolidated ASE and ASE Test Limited to
      better identify our investment targets. Also, in the efforts to keep in
      line with market trends to provide our customers with consistent and total
      solution services, we combined the packaging and testing units. The drop
      in total asset turnover rate was mainly due to massive increase in the
      long-term equity investment from the acquisition of ASE Test (increase in
      denominator) and huge decline in Q4 sales that led to significant drop in
      revenues (decrease in numerator). The combination of the two factors
      caused drop in the total asset turnover rate.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Lee
      X-ru, Shareholder No 624602: Question on change in&#160;&#160;the account
      of available-for-sale financial assets in consolidated balance sheet, the
      content of non-operating income, and the reason for the modified
      unqualified opinion issued by the CPA in financial
statements.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">CPA&#8217;s
      reply: Starting January 1, 2008, all listed companies must comply with the
      new regulations by expensing employee bonus and remuneration to directors
      and supervisors. The CPA must stress this matter when issuing an opinion.
      Thus </font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>

    <div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">7.
Matters for Discussions</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
      <div>
        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Item
1 (Proposed by the Board of Directors)</font></div>
      </div>
      <div>&#160;</div>
    </div>
    <div align="left">
      <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="15%">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Proposal:</font></div>
              </div>
            </td>
            <td valign="top" width="85%">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">To
      meet the requirements for larger production capacity in future the Company
      needs to enrich its operation capital in order to repay bank loans or the
      needs for other long-term development use, thereby enabling the
      fund-raising channels more diversified and flexible. As such, the
      shareholders&#8217; meeting is requested to authorize the board of directors to
      opt at the optimal time, depending on the market situation and the status
      of capital needs of the Company and in accordance with existing laws and
      regulations, for capital increase in cash by issuing common shares or
      joining the issuance of GDR (Global depository receipts) or domestic
      capital increase in cash or issuance of domestic or ECB to raise fund. The
      case is being presented for discussions.</font></div>
              </div>
            </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
            <td valign="top" width="85%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Explanation:</font></font></td>
            <td valign="top" width="85%">
              <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;
      </font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      principles to authorize the board of directors to issue new
      common</font></div>

        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">4</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div>&#160;</div>
    <div>&#160;</div>
    <div align="left">
      <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%">
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="15%">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
              </div>
            </td>
            <td valign="top" width="85%" style="PADDING-LEFT: 0pt">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">shares
      and GDR for capital increase in cash shall be as
      follows:</font></div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.1
      Issuance of common shares in the form GDR for capital increase in cash
      shall be limited to 500,000,000 shares only. The shareholders&#8217; meeting
      shall authorize the board of directors and the chairman of the board to
      make the adjustment by the market condition and issue the authorized GDR&#8217;s
      all at once.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.2
      In conducting issuance of new shares in the form of GDR for capital
      increase in cash, the issuance price shall be by the rules set forth in
      the Selfdiscipline Rules Concerning Subscription and Issuance of
      Securities by the Issuing Company Member Underwriters Have Assisted in the
      Process, i.e., the issuance price shall not be lower than the closing
      price of the Company&#8217;s common stock at the domestic open market. Take the
      simple arithmetic mean of the closing price of the common share on the
      first, third and fifth day prior to the price-setting day, minus 90% of
      the average stock price after gratuitous ex-rights and ex-interest, then
      comes the price for the new issue. However, the price-setting method may
      be duly adjusted if related domestic laws and regulations are updated.
      Since the stock price at home has often experience drastic volatility in
      the short run, the chairman of the board is authorized to set the actual
      issuance price within the above-mentioned price range, after having
      consulted with underwriter taking into consideration the international
      general practice, international capital market, domestic market price, the
      overall subscription status so as to make the offering price attractive to
      overseas investors. Consequently, the price-setting method should be
      reasonable. Additionally, the deciding method for the issuance price of
      GDR is based on the fair trading price of common shares at the domestic
      open market whereas the original stockholder may purchase the common
      shares at domestic stock exchange at the price close to the issuance price
      of the GDR, without bearing the exchange rate risk and liquidity risk.
      Moreover, the tranche of issuance of new shares and GRD for capital
      increase in cash do not affect much of the shareholders&#8217; equity as the
      highest dilution ratio in relation to the original shareholders&#8217; equity
      stands only at 9.14%.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.3
      10% of common shares issued for capital increase in cash shall, according
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">to
      Article 267 of The Company Act, be reserved for subscription by company
      employees and the remaining 90% will be fully appropriated for open
      issuance as the securities for GDR as the original shareholders have
      waived their rights for subscription in accordance with Article 28-1 of
      the Securities Trading Act. For the part that employees have not
      subscribed, the chairman of the board is authorized to contact specific
      party for purchase or, depending on the market requirements, list as the
      original securities for participation in the issuance of GDR.</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.4
      The proceeds for capital increase in cash from subscription to the GDR
      </font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>
      </table>

      be used for overseas procurement of materials, enrichment of operation
      capital, repayment of bank loans, purchase of machinery and equipment,
      and/or spin-off in one or multiple use and is expected to complete the
      implementation within 2 years after the fund is fully raised.
      Implementation of the said plan is expected to intensify the Company&#8217;s
      competitiveness, enhance the benefit of the operation efficiency,
      producing positive benefit to </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">shareholders.</font></div>
                    </div>

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.5
      The board of directors is authorized to set the major contents of the
      capital increase in cash plan, which includes issuance price, number of
      shares issued, issuance conditions, source of capital, plan items, amount
      of fund raised, estimated progress and estimated probable effect generated
      as well as the issuance plan of participation in the issuance of
      GDR.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.6
      Once the plan for capital increase in cash is approve d by the competent
      regulatory authority, the board of directors will be authorized to proceed
      with matters related to issuance of new shares.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.7
      If the agreement on issuance time, issuance condition, issuance volume,
      issuance amount of capital increase in cash and participation in issuance
      of GDR as well as other matters related to capital increase in cash and
      participation in issuance of GDR needs update in future due to the
      decision by the competent regulatory authority and on the basis of
      operation evaluation, or the needs of objective environment, the board of
      directors shall be authorized to handle at its full
      discretion.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.8
      In conjunction with the issuance method of common shares for capital
      increase in cash and participation in GDR issuance, the chairman of the
      board or his designated representative is authorized to represent the
      Company in signing all documents related to the participation in the
      issuance of GDR as well as handling all needed matters related to the
      participation in the issuance of GDR.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.9
      For matters that are not covered herein, the board of directors may, in
      accordance with law, proceed at its discretion.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;
      </font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The principles to authorize the

      Number of new shares issued for capital increase in cash shall not be in
      excess of 500,000,000 shares.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.2
      The par value of the new shares for capital increase in cash shall be
      NT$10 each. Actual issuance price shall be by related rules set forth in
      the</font></div>

      Rules Concerning Subscription and Issuance of Securities by the Issuing
      Company Member Underwriters Have Assisted in the Process and the market
      condition at the time of issuance. The chairman of she board and the

      The issuance method of new shares for the capital increase in cash shall
      be by price enquiry and selected purchase. With the exception of 10%-15%
      reserved for employees as required by Article 267 of The Company Act, the
      rest will be offered for public issuance as all original shareholders have
      waived their rights to subscribe according to Article 28-1 of the
      Securities Trading Act. In addition, if the Company&#8217;s employees have not
      subscribed sufficiently and adequately or waived the right to subscribe,
      the chairman may contact specific party for purchase.</font></div>
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

      The proceeds for capital increase in cash from subscription to the GDR
      shall be used for overseas procurement of materials, enrichment of
      operation capital, repayment of bank loans, purchase of machinery and
      equipment, and/or spin-off in one or multiple use and is expected to
      complete the implementation within 2 years after the fund is fully raised.
      Implementation of the said plan is expected to intensify the Company&#8217;s
      competitiveness, enhance the benefit of the operation efficiency,
      producing positive benefit to shareholders.</font></div>

      The board of directors is authorized to set the major contents of the
      capital increase in cash plan, which includes issuance price, number of
      shares issued, issuance conditions, plan items, amount of fund raised,
      estimated progress and estimated probable effect generated as well as the
      issuance plan of participation in the issuance of GDR.</font></div>

      Once the plan for capital increase in cash is approve d by the competent
      regulatory authority, the board of directors will be authorized to set the
      base date for capital increase.</font></div>

      With respect to the manner of issuance as mentioned in Section 2.3 above,
      the board of directors is authorized to make the amendment at its full
      discretion if amendment becomes necessary due to update of laws or
      regulations or the objective environment dictates the
      amendment.</font></div>

      For matters that are not covered herein, the board of directors may, in
      accordance with law, proceed at its discretion.</font></div>

      The proceeds from subscriptions to the domestic convertible corporate bond
      and ECB overseas shall be used for overseas procurement of materials,
      enrichment of operation capital, repayment of bank loans, purchase of
      machinery and equipment, and/or spin-off in one or multiple use and is

                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Acquisition
      or Disposal of Assets.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;
      &#160;For details of the table of comparison of the revised provisions of
      the Procedure for Acquisition or Disposal of Assets, please refer to
      Attachment IV to this Agenda Manual. Your consent is
      solicited.</font></div>
                </div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="15%">&#160;</td>
              <td valign="top" width="85%" style="PADDING-LEFT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="15%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;
    </font></td>
              <td valign="top" width="85%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Lu
      X-hui, Shareholder No.527934</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                </div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Shareholder
      Lu X-hui proposed the following: Except in the event of restructuring of
      the group organization or transfer or assignment between companies under
      the group, there are caps set for the total amounts of investment made by
      subsidiaries in marketable securities and individual security. When
      setting those caps, considerations could be given to the subsidiary&#8217;s own
      available funds and financial operation needs, and in addition, the
      Company&#8217;s net value provided in the financial statements that such
      investments should be capped at a certain percentage of the Company&#8217;s net
      value to ensure financial flexibility. Thus it is suggested that
      Subparagraph 2 and Subparagraph 3, Paragraph 1 of Article 4 of Procedure
      for the Company&#8217;s Acquisition or Disposal of Assets&#160;&#160;be revised
      as follows:</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#12302;</font>2. The
      Company&#8217;s total amount of marketable securities investments shall not
      exceed 150% of the net value on the Company&#8217;s&#8217; most recent financial
      reports.<font style="DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font>The total amount of
      marketable securities investments made by a subsidiary shall not exceed
      50% of the Company&#8217;s net value on the Company&#8217;s most recent financial
      reports.</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3.
      The amount of individual marketable security investment shall not exceed
      50% of the net value on the Company&#8217;s&#8217; most recent financial reports. The
      amount of investment in individual marketable security made by a
      subsidiary shall not exceed 20% of the Company&#8217;s net value on the
      Company&#8217;s most recent financial reports.<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#12303;</font></font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>

1 (Proposed by the Board of Directors)</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

                </div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="85%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Re-election
      of the Company&#8217;s directors and supervisors whose terms have
      expired</font></div>
                </div>
              </td>

              <td valign="top" width="15%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Explanation:</font></div>
                </div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="85%">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;In
      the current term, there are seven directors and five supervisors whose
      terms </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">expire
      on June 21, 2009, who should be reelected according to law.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                </div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;According
      to Article 16 of the Company&#8217;s Articles of Incorporation, the </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Company
      shall have seven to nine directors, of which two are independent
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">directors
      and five to seven are non-independent directors, and there are also to
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">be
      five to seven supervisors, with three-year terms.&#160;&#160;In this
      proposal, as resolved </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">by
      the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors Meeting on April 8, 2009, nine directors,
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">of
      which two are independent directors and seven are non-independent
      directors, </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">as
      well as five supervisors, are to be elected at this Shareholders&#8217; Meeting.
      The </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">terms
      of the new directors and supervisors will be for three years, from
      </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">June
      26, 2009, to June 25, 2012.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
                </div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">

      &#160;See below for the list of independent supervisor candidates and
      their information.</font></div>

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Explanation:</font></div>
                </div>

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;
      &#160; According to the stipulations of Article 209 of the Company Act,
      when a director take actions as part of the operations of their own
      company or the company of a third party, the director should explain the
      important details of these actions to the Shareholders&#8217; Meeting and
      receive their permission.</font></div>
                </div>

      &#160;&#160; It is planned to request the agreement of the Shareholders&#8217;
      Meeting to release the new directors and their representatives from the

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 324pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#9632;Attachment
I</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advanced
Semiconductor Engineering, Inc.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Business
Report</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2008 was
a year of intense shocks that will be hard to forget. The major shocks in all
kinds of raw material prices starting in the second half of 2007 made businesses
face the extreme tests of inventory and cost controls. Furthermore, a series of
financial crises caused by the subprime mortgage crisis caused the global
economy to freeze up. Faced with the biggest recession since the end of the
World War II, the international financial system bordered on collapse. Problems
such as the rapid climb of the unemployment rate, the fast drop in consumer
confidence, liquidity risk, and stagflation were piled one on top of the other.
The output value of the global semiconductor industry fell from US$267 billion
in 2007 to US$256 billion in 2008. According to the statistics of the ITRI&#8217;s IEK
ITIS project, the 2008 packaging industry output value in Taiwan was NT$221.7
billion, which was a 2.8% drop from 2007 and the first time in the seven yers
since 2001 that there was a drop in full year growth in the packaging industry.
In 2008, the testing industry output in Taiwan was NT$96.5 billion, which was a
5.7% drop from 2007.&#160;&#160;Faced with a poor outlook across the entire
global economy, the Company used this time to adjust its organizational system
and continue to concentrate on its industry while paying close attention to the
development of the financial storm in order to properly face the myriad changes
in these times. The following is our report on the company&#8217;s operation for the
past year:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Report
on Operations in Fiscal 2008</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Implementation
results of business plan for 2008</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Company&#8217;s combined revenues for 2008 were NT$94.4 billion, a drop of 6.7 billion
from 2007, a contraction of&#160;&#160;6.7%. After the government opened up
direct investment to the mainland and the three direct links in the second half
of last year, the Company took full advantage of this opportunity, actively
investing in China and searching for strategic alliances with international
customers to lower costs and also in expectation of creating yield with high
growth. In the second half of the year, the global economy greatly contracted,
and as large international companies all announced production cuts and even
financial problems, the Company faced these crises by raising operational
efficiency, merging product lines, and adjusting human resources. Amid the
intense fluctuations of the packaging and testing industry in 2008, the industry
managed to show a profit in the fourth quarter, so there was not a loss in the
forth quarter in main business area and profit in 2009. This shows the Company&#8217;s
ability to counter the effects of the industry cycle.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2.&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Budget
performance</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">No
financial forecast was disclosed in 2008.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3.&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Analysis
of financial accounts and profitability</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As of the
end of 2008, the Company had paid-in capital of NT$56,904,277 thousans, and
shareholders equity of NT$69,671,994 thousans, representing 56% of the Company&#8217;s
total assets of NT$123,931,246 thousands. Long-terms funds represented 389% of
fixed </font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">15</font></div>
        <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
          <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="HDR">
        <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">assets,
and the current ratio was 134%. These financial ratios were slightly down on the
previous year; however, the Company&#8217;s overall financial structure and solvency
remained sound. Operating profit and net profit after tax fell to NT$5,954,013
thousands and NT$6,160,051 thousands respectively. Both overall operating
results and profitability were slightly down on the previous year, due to the
impact of the global economic downturn.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">R&amp;D
overview</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
regards technology development and R&amp;D, 3D SiP technology has become the
technology of choice for small, lightweight semiconductor packaging. The main
technologies in this area include TSV, PoP, embedded technology and IPD. The
global trend is towards the leveraging of these technologies to integrate
various types of active and passive component, sensors and activators. The new
technologies successfully developed by the Company in 2008 included 45nm copper
process technology / ultra-low-k dielectric wafer high-lead flip-chip packaging
and wire bonding technology, 65nm copper process / low-k wafer lead-free
flip-chip packaging and wafer-level packaging technology, TSV (Through Silicon
Via) technology, Si Interposer technology, IPD passive component integration and
packaging technology, new copper bonding technology, Bluetooth module
technology, Wi-Fi module technology, and fan-out&#160;&#160;Map PoP technology.
In the future, the Company will continue to focus on the development of both
production equipment and advanced packaging technologies (such as flip-chip,
BGA, CSP and 3D SiP, etc.), thereby maintaining the Company&#8217;s status as a world
leader in IC assembly and testing.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Business
Plan for 2009 in summary</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Operating
policy</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.1
Provide customer with services of &#8220;ultimate quality&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.2
Create long-term and stable profits for the organization and
customers</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.3
Create prosperity with suppliers together</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.4
Develop employees to be elite in respective areas</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.5 Treat
employees &#8220;in a fair and reasonable manner&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.6
Provide employees with a &#8220;harmonious, happy and open&#8221; work
environment</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">1.7
Maintain flexibility in operations</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">2.&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Projects
sales volume and references</font></div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In light
of current industry dynamics, future market demand and ASE&#8217;s capacity, the
</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">projected
sales volume for 2009 is as follows:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt" align="left">
      <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="45%">
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="21%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-TOP: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 2px solid">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Item</font></div>
            </td>
            <td valign="top" width="24%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-TOP: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 2px solid">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Project
      Sales</font></div>
            </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td valign="top" width="21%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 2px solid">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Package</font></div>
            </td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" width="24%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 2px solid">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Approx.
      4.2 billion chips</font></div>
            </td>

            </td>
            <td align="left" valign="top" width="24%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Approx.

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">3.&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Important
production and sales policies</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
        <div id="FTR">
          <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">16</font></div>
          <div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
            <hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div id="HDR">
          <div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    </div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In recent
years, development trends in packaging technology have mainly developed in the
directions of electronic component high density, high I/O amount, low operating
power, surface component modulization, and mixed structurability. This makes
packaging technology go in the directions of high integration,
multi-pin/microtechnology, slimming, multichip module packaging, and low costs.
Because of the constantly growing demand by the industry for high-end packaging
capacity, ASE Group&#8217;s past investments in technology and capacity have prepared
it for these growing trends. In the future, we will continue to refine our
processes and also strive to enhance profitability.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Future
Development Strategy</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">According
to the estimates of ITRI&#8217;s IEK, the output value of the IC industry in Taiwan
and the global semiconductor industry will fall by 26.9% and 17.9% respectively
in 2009 compared to 2008. The stagnation in consumer confidence will cause
demand to drop dramatically, and it is expected that this will force companies
with poor organizational structures to declare bankruptcy or enter into mergers.
The asset-lite strategies of European and North American IDM companies will
accelerate the release of outsourcing orders later. By forming strategic
alliances with large international customers to increase demand and lower costs,
operating risks can be lowered after both parties become partners. The company
will maintain its financial robustness and also increase its cash on the books
in order to be able to take full advantage of opportunities in light of the
increasingly frequent mergers in the industry.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Influences
of external competitions, regulations and macroeconomics</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">After the
dramatic fluctuations of the price of oil in 2008, the energy problem will
receive ever-increasing attention from the market and will lead the next wave of
industry growth.&#160;&#160;Under the premise of maintaining the Company&#8217;s
operations and ensuring the interests of its shareholders, we will protect the
working rights and working opportunities of employees. In the future, when the
global outlook is pessimistic, the Company will still enhance its
competitiveness in expectation of being able to minimize the influence of the
external environment, constantly working for the shareholders and the
sustainable operation of the enterprise. When faced with challenges, we will
still boldly move forward in the hope that all shareholders can work together
with the Company to get through this hard time and build a better future
together.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

Jason C.S. Chang&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Manager:
Richard
H.P.&#160;&#160;Chang&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Accountant

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      4 Maximum amount of loans</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Loans
      may only be made out of the Company&#8217;s own capital and working capital, and
      may only be made if they are not prejudicial to the Company&#8217;s operational
      needs. The maximum size of loans shall be as follows:</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -6.6pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Cumulative total of all loans: The cumulative value of all loans made may
      not exceed 50% of the Company&#8217;s net worth in the most recent period. Loans
      made to companies or other businesses to meet short-term funding needed
      may not exceed 40% of the Company&#8217;s net worth.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Maximum size of loans made to an individual company or
      business:</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Loans made because of business dealings with the company or business
      concerned: Such loans may not exceed 20% of the Company&#8217;s net worth in the
      most recent period. Furthermore, because of risk management
      considerations, the loan size should not exceed the combined value of the
      transactions between the Company and the company or business in question
      over the past year.</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">(2)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Loans made to meet short-term funding needs may not exceed 20% of the
      Company&#8217;s net worth in the most recent period.</font></div>
                </td>

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      A floating interest rate shall apply to cash loans, to be adjusted in
      accordance with the Company&#8217;s funding costs. The Finance Office will
      submit all proposals for interest rate adjustment to the President for
      approval; interest shall be paid calculated on a monthly

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article 8
      Alterations to loans</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">If
      there are changes in the objective environment after a capital loan is

                <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px">

                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      8 Alterations to loans</font></div>
                  <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">If
      there are changes in the objective environment after a capital loan is
      made that cause <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">the recipient to not
      meet the stipulations of these handling procedures or</font> </font>the
      loan amount to exceed the limit, an improvement plan should be drafted and
      submitted to the supervisors<font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">, and improvements
      should be completed according to the plan&#8217;s
  schedule</font></font></div>
                </td>

      debt reserve. The Company should disclose all relevant information in its

                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      12 Procedures for the control of loans made by the Company&#8217;s subsidiaries
      to third parties</font></div>
                        <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">If
      a subsidiary of the Company plans to make a capital loan to a third party,
      the subsidiary should still draft a handling procedure for loans to third
      parties according to the stipulations of the Regulations Governing Loaning
      of Funds and Making of Endorsements/Guarantees by Public Companies issued
      by the Securities and Futures Institute.</font></div>
                      </td>

                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">debt
      reserve. The Company should disclose all relevant information in its
      financial statements, and should provide the Company&#8217;s Auditor with
      relevant information so that all relevant auditing procedures can be
      properly implemented.</font></div>
                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      12 Procedures for the control of loans made by the Company&#8217;s subsidiaries
      to third parties</font></div>
                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      If a subsidiary of the Company plans to make a capital loan to a third
      party, <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">the Company should
      order</font> </font>the subsidiary to draft a handling procedure for loans
      to third parties according to the stipulations of the Regulations
      Governing Loaning of Funds and Making of Endorsements/Guarantees by Public
      Companies issued by the <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">FSC</font>, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">and it should be
      handled according to the drafted handling
      procedure.</font></font></font></div>
                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      The total loans made by a subsidiary may not exceed 40% of the
      subsidiary&#8217;s net value as given on its most recent financial statements;
      loans to any individual company or business may not exceed 20% of the
      subsidiary&#8217;s net value.</font></td>
                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      The total loans made by a subsidiary may not exceed 40% of the
      subsidiary&#8217;s net value as given on its most recent financial statements;
      loans to any individual company or business may not exceed 20% of the
      subsidiary&#8217;s net value.</font></td>
                    </tr>

                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
                    </tr>

      Each subsidiary must, by the 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font>
      day of each month, compiled a list giving details of all loans made to
      third parties in the previous month, and must submit the list to the
      Company.</font></td>
                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Each subsidiary must, by the 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super; TEXT-DECORATION: none">th</font>
      day of each month, compiled a list giving details of all loans made to
      third parties in the previous month, and must submit the list to the
      Company.</font></td>

                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: 4px"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>

                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Each subsidiary&#8217;s internal auditing personnel should, at least once every
      quarter, conduct an audit of the procedures for and implementation status
      of the subsidiary&#8217;s granting of loans to third parties, and keep a written
      record of this audit. If any major violations are discovered, the internal
      auditing personnel should immediately notify the subsidiary&#8217;s
      supervisors</font></div>
                      </td>
                      <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; PADDING-LEFT: 0pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">

                        <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Each subsidiary&#8217;s internal auditing personnel should, at least once every
      quarter, conduct an audit of the procedures for and implementation status
      of the subsidiary&#8217;s granting of loans to third parties, and keep a written
      record of this audit. If any major violations are discovered, the internal
      auditing personnel should immediately notify the subsidiary&#8217;s supervisors
      in writing, </font></div>

      firm that controls over 50% of the voting rights in the Company (either
      directly or indirectly).</font></div>

              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article

      The Company may only provide endorsements for the following:</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">(1)&#160;&#160;
      Firms with which the Company has business dealings.</font></div>

            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-TOP: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Original
      Provisions</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-TOP: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: #000000 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Provisions
      after Revision</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      7 Exceeding the limits set for endorsements and guarantees, and alteration
      of endorsements and guarantees</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      &#160;&#160;Where operational requirements make it necessary for the
      Company to exceed the limits specified in Article 4 above when providing
      endorsements or guarantees, this must be approved by the board of
      directors, and at least 50% of the members of the board of directors must
      sign a joint guarantee to make good any loss that the Company may suffer
      as a result; furthermore, the Operational Procedures for Endorsements and
      Guarantees must be revised and submitted to the Shareholders Meeting for
      retroactive approval. If the Shareholders Meeting does not agree to the
      revision, then plans must be drawn up to eliminate the excess amount
      within a specified time limit. If the Company has appointed Independent
      Directors, then full consideration should be given to the views of these
      Independent Directors when the matter is being discussed by the Board of
      Directors; whether the Independent Directors agree or disagree (and the
      reasons for their disagreement in the latter case) should be recorded in
      the minutes of the board meeting.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      7 Exceeding the limits set for endorsements and guarantees, and alteration
      of endorsements and guarantees</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      &#160;&#160;&#160;Where operational requirements make it necessary for the
      Company to exceed the limits specified in Article 4 above when providing
      endorsements or guarantees, this must be approved by the board of
      directors, and at least 50% of the members of the board of directors must
      sign a joint guarantee to make good any loss that the Company may suffer
      as a result; furthermore, the Operational Procedures for Endorsements and
      Guarantees must be revised and submitted to the Shareholders Meeting for
      retroactive approval. If the Shareholders Meeting does not agree to the
      revision, then plans must be drawn up to eliminate the excess amount
      within a specified time limit. If the Company has appointed Independent
      Directors, then full consideration should be given to the views of these
      Independent Directors when the matter is being discussed by the Board of
      Directors; whether the Independent Directors agree or disagree (and the
      reasons for their disagreement in the latter case) should be recorded in
      the minutes of the board meeting.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;
    </font></td>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">&#160;
    </font></td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      When recipients of the Company&#8217;s endorsements originally meet the
      stipulations of Article 3 and then fail to meet them later,&#160;&#160;or
      when the&#160;&#160;endorsement amount exceeds the amount set in Article 4
      because of a basic change in the calculated limit, this recipient&#8217;s
      endorsement amount or the excessive portion should be fully canceled when
      the contract term expires or within a certain period of time in a
      separately agreed upon plan, and the related improvement plan should be
      submitted to the supervisors.</font></div>
              </td>
              <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      When recipients of the Company&#8217;s endorsements originally meet the
      stipulations of Article 3 and then fail to meet them later,&#160;&#160;or
      when the&#160;&#160;endorsement amount exceeds the amount set in Article 4
      because of a basic change in the calculated limit, <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">an improvement plan
      should be set for</font> </font>this recipient&#8217;s endorsement amount or the
      excessive portion, the related improvement plan should be submitted to the
      supervisors, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">and
      improvements should be completed ccording to the plan&#8217;s
      schedule.</font></font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      9:&#160; Disclosure of endorsements and guarantees</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      &#160;&#160;The Company shall, by the 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font>
      day of each month, make a public announcement of the total amount of
      endorsements and guarantees provided by the Company and its subsidiaries
      in the previous month</font></div>
              </td>
              <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      9:&#160; Disclosure of endorsements and guarantees</font></div>
                <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: -27pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The
      Company shall, by the 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font>
      day of each month, make a public announcement of the total amount of
      endorsements and guarantees provided by the Company and its subsidiaries
      in the previous month</font></div>

      report after making a public announcement according to this

      The Company shall undertake a quarterly appraisal and writing down of all
      contingent loss deriving from endorsements and guarantees, in accordance
      with the provisions of the Financial Reporting Standards Gazette No. 9,
      and shall appropriate disclosure of such contingent loss in its financial
      statements; the Company shall also provide its Auditor with relevant

      and shall appropriate disclosure of such contingent loss in its financial
      statements; the Company shall also provide its Auditor with relevant

  procedures.</font></div>
