                <tr>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      11 Procedure for the Control of Handling of Endorsements by
      Subsidiaries</font></div>
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      If a subsidiary of the Company plans to endorse a third party or provide
      an endorsement, the subsidiary should still draft a handling procedure for
      endorsements and guarantees according to the stipulations of the
      Regulations Governing Loaning of Funds and Making of
      Endorsements/Guarantees by Public Companies issued by the Securities &amp;
      Futures Information Center.</font></div>
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                  </td>
                  <td align="left" valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">Article
      11 Procedure for the Control of Handling of Endorsements by
      Subsidiaries</font></div>
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">1.&#160;&#160;
      &#160;&#160;If a subsidiary of the Company plans to endorse a third party
      or provide an endorsement, <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">the Company should
      order</font> </font>the subsidiary to draft a handling procedure for
      endorsements and guarantees according to the stipulations of the
      Regulations Governing Loaning of Funds and Making of
      Endorsements/Guarantees by Public Companies issued by the <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">FSC</font>, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">and it should be
      handled according to the drafted handling
      procedure.</font></font></font></div>
                  </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;
      &#160;The total amount of endorsements and guarantees provided by a
      subsidiary may not exceed 100% of the subsidiary&#8217;s net worth as given in
      its most recent financial statements; endorsements and guarantees provided
      to any individual firm may not exceed 70% of the subsidiary&#8217;s net
      worth.</font></div>
                  </td>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">2.&#160;&#160;
      &#160;The total amount of endorsements and guarantees provided by a
      subsidiary may not exceed 100% of the subsidiary&#8217;s net worth as given in
      its most recent financial statements; endorsements and guarantees provided
      to any individual firm may not exceed 70% of the subsidiary&#8217;s net
      worth.</font></div>
                  </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Each subsidiary shall, by the 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font>
      day of each month, compile a list of all endorsements and guarantees
      provided in the previous month, and shall submit the list to the
      Company.</font></div>
                  </td>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">3.&#160;&#160;
      &#160;&#160;Each subsidiary shall, by the 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font>
      day of each month, compile a list of all endorsements and guarantees
      provided in the previous month, and shall submit the list to the
      Company.</font></div>
                  </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
      Each subsidiary&#8217;s internal auditing personnel should, at least once every
      quarter, conduct an audit of the procedures for and implementation status
      of the subsidiary&#8217;s granting of endorsements and guarantees, and keep a
      written record of this audit. If any major violations are discovered, the
      internal auditing personnel should immediately notify the subsidiary&#8217;s
      supervisors in</font></div>
                  </td>
                  <td valign="top" width="50%" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">
                    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: -1.3pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;
      &#160;Each subsidiary&#8217;s internal auditing personnel should, at least once
      every quarter, conduct an audit of the procedures for and implementation
      status of the subsidiary&#8217;s granting of endorsements and guarantees, and
      keep a written record of this audit. If any major violations are
      discovered, the internal auditing personnel should immediately notify the
      subsidiary&#8217;s</font></div>
                  </td>
                </tr>
            </table>

      24</font></div>
              <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">The
      Company is currently in the business growth stage. To meet the capital
      needs for business development now and in the future and satisfy the
      requirements of shareholders for cash inflow, the Company&#8217;s dividend
      policy shall use residual dividend policy to distribute dividends, of
      which the cash dividend distribution rate is 0%&#8211;50% of the total dividend
      amount, with the remainder to be distributed as stock dividends. However,
      depending on factors such as the economic situation, business development,
      and cash position holdings, the Company shall adjust the cash dividend and
      stock dividend distribution rate when necessary with a surplus
      distribution plan made by the Board of Directors and passed by resolution
      of the Shareholders&#8217; Meeting.</font></div>

      future and satisfy the requirements of shareholders for cash inflow, the

      dividends, of which the <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">cash dividend

      dividends. A surplus distribution plan is also to be made by the Board of
      Directors and passed by resolution of the Shareholders&#8217;
      Meeting.</font></div>
